                  <AssemblerScript>//AI Help me write a cheat engine lua script that creates a form that takes a user string input and displays some basic information
{$lua}
[ENABLE]
-- Clean up existing form if it exists
if UE.TestForm then
  UE.TestForm.close()
end

-- Create the main form
UE.TestForm = createForm()
UE.TestForm.Caption = "Part String Input Form"
UE.TestForm.Width = 400
UE.TestForm.Height = 300
UE.TestForm.Position = "poScreenCenter"

-- Create input label
local inputLabel = createLabel(UE.TestForm)
inputLabel.Caption = "Enter Part String:"
inputLabel.Left = 20
inputLabel.Top = 20
inputLabel.Width = 100

-- Create input field
local inputEdit = createEdit(UE.TestForm)
inputEdit.Left = 20
inputEdit.Top = 45
inputEdit.Width = 340
inputEdit.Height = 25
inputEdit.Text="Parts";
UE.TestForm.EditBox=inputEdit;

-- Create submit button
local submitButton = createButton(UE.TestForm)
submitButton.Caption = "Submit"
submitButton.Left = 20
submitButton.Top = 80
submitButton.Width = 100
submitButton.Height = 30

-- Create info display area
local infoMemo = createMemo(UE.TestForm)
infoMemo.Left = 20
infoMemo.Top = 120
infoMemo.Width = 340
infoMemo.Height = 120
infoMemo.ReadOnly = true
infoMemo.ScrollBars = "ssVertical"
infoMemo.append("Item Info:");

-- Button click event handler
submitButton.OnClick = function()
  local userInput = inputEdit.Text
  if userInput == "" then
    return
  end
  UE.TestForm.close();
end

-- Allow Enter key to submit
inputEdit.OnKeyUp = function(sender, key)
  if key == VK_RETURN then
    submitButton.OnClick()
return false;
  end
end

-- Create clear button
local clearButton = createButton(UE.TestForm)
clearButton.Caption = "Clear"
clearButton.Left = 130
clearButton.Top = 80
clearButton.Width = 100
clearButton.Height = 30

clearButton.OnClick = function()
  inputEdit.Text = ""
  infoMemo.Text = ""
  inputEdit.setFocus()
end
UE.TestForm.OnClose=function();
  UE.TestForm.destroy()
  UE.TestForm = nil
  memrec.Active=false;
end
-- Show the form
UE.TestForm.show()

[DISABLE]
if UE.TestForm then
  UE.TestForm.close()
end
</AssemblerScript>

{$asm}
alloc(FPSFixInjection,$1000,FPSFixMEM)
label(FPSFixInjectionAllowed return)
FPSFixInjection:
add rsp,00000230
cmp [FPSFixInjectionAllowed],0
je return
jmp FPSFixMEM

FPSFixInjectionAllowed:
dq 0

FPSFixMEM+F:
  jmp FPSFixInjection
  nop 2
return:
registersymbol( FPSFixInjection FPSFixInjectionAllowed)

if not B then;
return;

writeBytes(FPSFixMEM+0xF,{0x48,0x81,0xC4,0x30,0x02,0,0})

local THREAD_ALL_ACCESS = 0x001F03FF
local ThreadQuerySetWin32StartAddress = 0x9

local thread_id
local thread_handle
local dwStartAddress = allocateMemory( 0x1000 )
local nt_status

local module_base = getAddressSafe( process )
local func_addr = module_base +0x21e18265-- 0x21607AE3
for i = 1, tl.Count - 1 do
  thread_id = tonumber( tl[i], 16 )
  thread_handle = executeCodeEx( 0, nil, OpenThread, THREAD_ALL_ACCESS, 0, thread_id )
  nt_status = executeCodeEx( 0, nil, NtQueryInformationThread, thread_handle, ThreadQuerySetWin32StartAddress, dwStartAddress, 0x8, 0 )
  if nt_status == 0x0 then
    if readQword( dwStartAddress ) == func_addr then
      local t = executeCodeEx( 0, nil, TerminateThread, thread_handle, 0 )
      executeCodeEx( 0, nil, CloseHandle, thread_handle )
      showMessage( string.format( "Symbiote thread with id: 0x%X killed.", thread_id ) )
      break
    end
  end
  executeCodeEx( 0, nil, CloseHandle, thread_handle )
end

deAlloc( dwStartAddress )

printf("Debug Prevention Opcode01: %X",AOB);
writeBytes(AOB+0x5,{0x8A,0x11});

[ENABLE]
aobscanmodule(ChallengeInstruction,Borderlands4.exe,48 89 44 24 20 48 89 F9 4C 8B 44 24 ?? 4C 8B 8C 24 ?? ?? ?? ?? E8)
alloc(ChallengeHook,$1000,ChallengeInstruction)
label(return ChallengeCompleter ChallengeCompleterEnd ChallengeCompleterSecond CheckForChallenge)

ChallengeHook:
mov r9,[rsp+000000B8]
mov r8,0

ChallengeCompleter:
//Get Max Value
mov rax,[r9+8]
cmp rax,0
jbe ChallengeCompleterEnd
//Get Current Value
mov rcx,[r9]
cmp rcx,rax
ja ChallengeCompleterEnd
//lower max by 1
add rax,-1
//Set Value
mov [r9],rax

cmp r8,0
ja ChallengeCompleterSecond

ChallengeCompleterEnd:
//Go Back Till Previous Challenge
add r9,-20
mov rcx,[r9]
add r9,8
cmp rcx,[CheckForChallenge]
jae ChallengeCompleter
cmp rcx,1
je ChallengeCompleter
add r8,1

ChallengeCompleterSecond:
//Go Forward To Next Challenge
add r9,10
mov rcx,[r9]
add r9,8
cmp rcx,[CheckForChallenge]
jae ChallengeCompleter
//cmp rcx,1
//je ChallengeCompleter


mov rax,[rsp+20]
mov rcx,rdi
mov r8,[rsp+70]
mov r9,[rsp+000000B8]
jmp return

CheckForChallenge:
dq FFFFFFFF00000000

ChallengeInstruction+D:
  jmp ChallengeHook
  nop 3
return:

  registersymbol(ChallengeInstruction ChallengeHook ChallengeCompleter ChallengeCompleterEnd ChallengeCompleterSecond CheckForChallenge)
[DISABLE]
ChallengeInstruction+D:
db 4C 8B 8C 24 B8 00 00 00

unregistersymbol(ChallengeInstruction ChallengeCompleter ChallengeCompleterEnd ChallengeCompleterSecond CheckForChallenge)
dealloc(ChallengeHook)

[ENABLE]
function createHeader(parent, name)
    local hdr = getAddressList().createMemoryRecord()
    hdr.isGroupHeader = true
    hdr.Description = name
    hdr.appendToEntry(parent)
    return hdr
end

function createEntry(group, desc, offset)
    local e = getAddressList().createMemoryRecord()
    e.Description = desc
    e.Address = "GEngine+1358"
    e.Type = vtDword
    e.ShowAsSigned = false
    e.setOffsetCount(6)
    e.Offset[0] = offset
    e.Offset[1] = 0x6D58
    e.Offset[2] = 0x3D0
    e.Offset[3] = 0x30
    e.Offset[4] = 0x0
    e.Offset[5] = 0x38
    e.appendToEntry(group)
end

UE.TimerFunctions.Add("FullWeaponMods",function();
local Ammo=getAddressSafe("[[[[GEngine+0x1358]+0x38]+0]+0x30]");

writeByte(Ammo+0x2558,1);--Ammo
Ammo=readPointer(Ammo+0x3D0);
if Ammo then;
WriteFloat(Ammo+0x4A98,9999999999);--Damage
writeByte(Ammo+0x6524,1);--CanUseWhileSprinting
writeByte(Ammo+0x6530,1);--CanZoomWhileSprinting

WriteFloat(Ammo+0x2C0,0);--FirstShotOffsetScale
WriteFloat(Ammo+0x2C8,0);--RecoilScale
WriteFloat(Ammo+0x2BC,0);--RecoilScaleY
WriteFloat(Ammo+0x2B8,0);--RecoilScaleX
WriteFloat(Ammo+0x388,3);--Projectile Speed Scale
end
Ammo=getAddressSafe("[[[[[[[GEngine+0x1358]+0x38]+0]+0x30]+0xA08]+0x5FF0]+0x20]+0x74");--FireRate
if Ammo then;WriteFloat(Ammo,5);end
end
end
end);

              <AssemblerScript Async="1">{$lua}
local Ofs_Movement=getAddressSafe("Character.CharacterMovement");
local Ofs_JumpCurrentCount=getAddressSafe("Character.JumpCurrentCount");

local Ofs_GravityScale=getAddressSafe("CharacterMovementComponent.GravityScale");
local Ofs_WalkableFloorAngle=getAddressSafe("CharacterMovementComponent.WalkableFloorAngle");
local Ofs_WalkableFloorZ=getAddressSafe("CharacterMovementComponent.WalkableFloorZ");
local Ofs_MaxStepHeight=getAddressSafe("CharacterMovementComponent.MaxStepHeight");
local Ofs_AirControl=getAddressSafe("CharacterMovementComponent.AirControl");
local Ofs_AirControlBoostMultiplier=getAddressSafe("CharacterMovementComponent.AirControlBoostMultiplier");
local Ofs_AirControlBoostVelocityThreshold=getAddressSafe("CharacterMovementComponent.AirControlBoostVelocityThreshold");

local Ofs_VaultPowerCost_Dash=getAddressSafe("OakCharacterMovementComponent.VaultPowerCost_Dash");
local Ofs_VaultPowerCost_Glide=getAddressSafe("OakCharacterMovementComponent.VaultPowerCost_Glide");
[ENABLE]
UE.TimerFunctions.Add("FullMovementMods",function();
local PawnComp=getAddressSafe("LocalPlayerPawn");
if PawnComp then;
local StateComp=getAddressSafe("[[LocalPlayerPawn+0x168]+0x398]");
if ReadByte(StateComp+0xDF2)==0 then
writeInteger(PawnComp+Ofs_JumpCurrentCount,0);
PawnComp=readPointer(PawnComp+Ofs_Movement);
if PawnComp then;
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_GravityScale,0.5);
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_WalkableFloorAngle,120)
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_WalkableFloorZ,0.1)
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_MaxStepHeight,90)--MaxStepHeight
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_AirControl,2)---AirControl
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_AirControlBoostMultiplier,5)---AirControlBoostMultiplier
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_AirControlBoostVelocityThreshold,42)---AirControlBoostVelocityThreshold
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_VaultPowerCost_Dash+4,0)---VaultPowerCost_Dash
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_VaultPowerCost_Glide+4,0)---VaultPowerCost_Glide
end
else

PawnComp=readPointer(PawnComp+Ofs_Movement);
if PawnComp then;
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_GravityScale,0);
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_GravityScale,1);
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_WalkableFloorAngle,44.76508331)
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_WalkableFloorZ,0.7099999785)
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_MaxStepHeight,45)--MaxStepHeight
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_AirControl,0.6000000238)---AirControl
end

end
end
end);
[DISABLE]
UE.TimerFunctions.Remove("FullMovementMods");
local PawnComp=getAddressSafe("LocalPlayerPawn");
if PawnComp then;
PawnComp=readPointer(PawnComp+Ofs_Movement);
if PawnComp then;
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_GravityScale,1);
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_WalkableFloorAngle,44.76508331)
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_WalkableFloorZ,0.7099999785)
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_MaxStepHeight,45)--MaxStepHeight
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_AirControl,0.6000000238)---AirControl
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_AirControlBoostMultiplier,2)---AirControlBoostMultiplier
--writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_AirControlBoostVelocityThreshold,25)---AirControlBoostVelocityThreshold
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_VaultPowerCost_Dash+4,50)---VaultPowerCost_Dash
writeFloat(PawnComp+Ofs_VaultPowerCost_Glide+4,15)---VaultPowerCost_Glide
end
end

              <VariableType>Auto Assembler Script</VariableType>
              <AssemblerScript Async="1">{$lua}
local moveSpeed = 140;
local PawnComp,yaw,pitch,yawRad,pitchRad,MX,MY,MZ=nil;
[ENABLE]
UE.Noclip_X,UE.Noclip_Y,UE.Noclip_Z,UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent=nil,nil,nil,nil;
UE.TimerFunctions.Add("Noclip",function()
PawnComp=getAddressSafe("[LocalPlayerPawn+Character.CharacterMovement]+CharacterMovementComponent.GravityScale");
if PawnComp then;writeFloat(PawnComp,0);else
  print("Noclip Failed");
  UE.TimerFunctions.Remove("Noclip");
return;
end
UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent=getAddressSafe("[LocalPlayerPawn+Actor.RootComponent]");
UE.LocalPlayerComponent=getAddressSafe("LocalPlayerController");
if UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent then
  if not UE.Noclip_X or not UE.Noclip_Y or not UE.Noclip_Z then
    UE.Noclip_X=readDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x260);
    UE.Noclip_Y=readDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x268);
    UE.Noclip_Z=readDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x270);
  end
  if not UE.Noclip_X or not UE.Noclip_Y or not UE.Noclip_Z then
    print("Error Noclip Position Invalid");
    return;
  end
yaw = readDouble(UE.LocalPlayerComponent+0x410);
pitch = readDouble(UE.LocalPlayerComponent+0x408);
yawRad,pitchRad = math.rad(yaw),math.rad(pitch);
if isKeyPressed(VK_W) then
MX = math.cos(pitchRad) * math.cos(yawRad);
MY = math.cos(pitchRad) * math.sin(yawRad);
MZ = math.sin(pitchRad);
UE.Noclip_X = UE.Noclip_X + (MX * moveSpeed);
UE.Noclip_Y = UE.Noclip_Y + (MY * moveSpeed);
UE.Noclip_Z = UE.Noclip_Z + (MZ * moveSpeed);
elseif isKeyPressed(VK_S) then
MX = math.cos(pitchRad) * math.cos(yawRad);
MY = math.cos(pitchRad) * math.sin(yawRad);
MZ = math.sin(pitchRad);
UE.Noclip_X = UE.Noclip_X - (MX * moveSpeed);
UE.Noclip_Y = UE.Noclip_Y - (MY * moveSpeed);
UE.Noclip_Z = UE.Noclip_Z - (MZ * moveSpeed);
end

if isKeyPressed(VK_A) then
MX =-math.sin(yawRad);
MY = math.cos(yawRad);
UE.Noclip_X = UE.Noclip_X - (MX * moveSpeed);
UE.Noclip_Y = UE.Noclip_Y - (MY * moveSpeed);
elseif isKeyPressed(VK_D) then
MX =-math.sin(yawRad);
MY = math.cos(yawRad);
UE.Noclip_X = UE.Noclip_X + (MX * moveSpeed);
UE.Noclip_Y = UE.Noclip_Y + (MY * moveSpeed);
end

  if isKeyPressed(VK_SPACE) then;UE.Noclip_Z = UE.Noclip_Z + moveSpeed;end
  if isKeyPressed(VK_LSHIFT) then;UE.Noclip_Z = UE.Noclip_Z - moveSpeed;end
  writeDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x260,UE.Noclip_X);-- writeDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x198,UE.Noclip_X);
  writeDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x268,UE.Noclip_Y);-- writeDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x1A0,UE.Noclip_Y);
  writeDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x270,UE.Noclip_Z);-- writeDouble(UE.LocalPlayerPawnRootComponent+0x1A8,UE.Noclip_Z);
else
PawnComp=getAddressSafe("[LocalPlayerPawn+Character.CharacterMovement]+CharacterMovementComponent.GravityScale");
if PawnComp then;writeFloat(PawnComp,1);end
print("Noclip Failed");
UE.TimerFunctions.Remove("Noclip");
end
end);
[DISABLE]
UE.TimerFunctions.Remove("Noclip");
PawnComp=getAddressSafe("[LocalPlayerPawn+Character.CharacterMovement]+CharacterMovementComponent.GravityScale");
if PawnComp then;writeFloat(PawnComp,1);end
</AssemblerScript>

              <ID>1337325311</ID>
              <Description>"Print All Enemys (Filtered)"</Description>
              <LastState/>
              <VariableType>Auto Assembler Script</VariableType>
              <AssemblerScript Async="1">{$lua}
[ENABLE]
CreateThread(function()
local Level=GetAddressSafe("[[[GEngine+0xC20]+0x78]+0x30]");
if not Level then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The Level");
return
end
local B=readInteger(Level+0xA8);
local A=readPointer(Level+0xA0);
local C=0;
local D=0;
local E=0;
local F=0;
for C=0,B,1 do
D=readPointer(A+(0x8*C));
if D and UE.IsPlayerType(D) then
E=UE.GetName(readInteger(D+0x18));
--Get Team Name
F=ReadPointer(D+0x880)
F=F and ReadPointer(F+0x8) or nil
F=F and readInteger(F+0xC) or nil
F=F and UE.GetName(F) or nil;
if F and F~="Team_Player" then
printf("0x%X -&gt; %s -&gt; %s",D,E or "Unknown Entity",F or "Unknown Team");
end
end
end
memrec.Active = false;
end)
[DISABLE]
</AssemblerScript>
            </CheatEntry>

              <AssemblerScript>{$lua}
[ENABLE]
CreateThread(function()
local Level=GetAddressSafe("[[[GEngine+0xC20]+0x78]+0x30]");
if not Level then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The Level");
return
end
local LocalPlayer=getAddressSafe("[[[[[GEngine+0x1358]+0x38]]+0x30]+0x3D0]");
if not LocalPlayer then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The LocalPlayer");
return
end
local LocalPlayerRootComponent=readPointer(LocalPlayer+0x1C8);
local LocalPlayerX,LocalPlayerY,LocalPlayerZ=readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x260),readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x268),readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x270);
local B=readInteger(Level+0xA8);
local A=readPointer(Level+0xA0);
local C=0;
local D=0;
local E=0;
for C=0,B,1 do
D=readPointer(A+(0x8*C));
if D and D~=LocalPlayer and UE.IsPlayerType(D) then
E=readPointer(D+0x1C8);
if E then
writeDouble(E+0x260,LocalPlayerX);
writeDouble(E+0x268,LocalPlayerY);
writeDouble(E+0x270,LocalPlayerZ+84);
local X,Y,Z=readDouble(E+0x260),readDouble(E+0x268),readDouble(E+0x270);
E=UE.GetName(readInteger(D+0x18));
--printf("0x%X -&gt; %s , X: %f, Y: %f, Z: %f",D,E or "Unknown Entity",X,Y,Z);
end
end
end
memrec.Active = false;
end)

if not Level then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The Level");
return
end
local LocalPlayer=getAddressSafe("[[[[[GEngine+0x1358]+0x38]]+0x30]+0x3D0]");
local LocalPlayerController=getAddressSafe("LocalPlayerController");
if not LocalPlayer or not LocalPlayerController then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The LocalPlayer");
return
end
local B=readInteger(Level+0xA8);
local A=readPointer(Level+0xA0);
local C=0;
local D=0;
local E=0;
for C=0,B,1 do
D=readPointer(A+(0x8*C));
if D and D~=LocalPlayer and UE.IsPlayerType(D) then
writeFloat(D+0x74,20);
writeFloat(D+0x4318,999999999);
writeByte(D+0x431C,1);
writePointer(D+0x4488,LocalPlayer);
writePointer(D+0x4380,LocalPlayer);
writePointer(D+0x4C50,LocalPlayer);
writePointer(D+0x4310,LocalPlayerController);
writePointer(D+0x4378,LocalPlayerController);
writePointer(D+0x4488,LocalPlayerController);
writePointer(D+0x3B8,LocalPlayerController);
UE.ReadResourcePools(D,function(B,C,N);
if N=="Resource_AI_Health_01" or N=="Resource_AI_Health_02" then
writeFloat(C+0xC8,0);
end
end);
end
end
memrec.Active = false;
end)

              <ID>1337325695</ID>
              <Description>"Tp All To Local Player (Crosshair)"</Description>
              <LastState/>
              <VariableType>Auto Assembler Script</VariableType>
              <AssemblerScript>{$lua}
[ENABLE]
local crosshairDistance = 500; -- Adjust this distance as needed (units in front of player)
CreateThread(function()
local Level=GetAddressSafe("[[[GEngine+0xC20]+0x78]+0x30]");
if not Level then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The Level");
return
end
local LocalPlayer=getAddressSafe("[[[[[GEngine+0x1358]+0x38]]+0x30]+0x3D0]");
if not LocalPlayer then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The LocalPlayer");
return
end
local LocalPlayerRootComponent=readPointer(LocalPlayer+0x1C8);
local LocalPlayerX,LocalPlayerY,LocalPlayerZ=readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x260),readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x268),readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x270);

-- Read player camera rotation for crosshair calculation
local yaw = readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x1B8);   -- Yaw (Z-axis rotation)
local pitch = readDouble(LocalPlayerRootComponent+0x1B0); -- Pitch (Y-axis rotation)

-- Convert to radians for math functions
local yawRad = math.rad(yaw);
local pitchRad = math.rad(pitch);

-- Calculate crosshair direction vector
local forwardX = math.cos(pitchRad) * math.cos(yawRad);
local forwardY = math.cos(pitchRad) * math.sin(yawRad);
local forwardZ = -math.sin(pitchRad);

-- Calculate crosshair world position
local crosshairX = LocalPlayerX + (forwardX * crosshairDistance);
local crosshairY = LocalPlayerY + (forwardY * crosshairDistance);
local crosshairZ = LocalPlayerZ + (forwardZ * crosshairDistance);

local B=readInteger(Level+0xA8);
local A=readPointer(Level+0xA0);
local C=0;
local D=0;
local E=0;
for C=0,B,1 do
D=readPointer(A+(0x8*C));
if D and D~=LocalPlayer and UE.IsPlayerType(D) then
E=readPointer(D+0x1C8);
if E then
-- Teleport to crosshair position instead of player position
writeDouble(E+0x260,crosshairX);
writeDouble(E+0x268,crosshairY);
writeDouble(E+0x270,crosshairZ);
local X,Y,Z=readDouble(E+0x260),readDouble(E+0x268),readDouble(E+0x270);
E=UE.GetName(readInteger(D+0x18));
--printf("0x%X -&gt; %s , X: %f, Y: %f, Z: %f",D,E or "Unknown Entity",X,Y,Z);
end
end
end
memrec.Active = false;
end)

label(p_item p_iinfo return)
newmem:
  mov [p_iinfo],r14
  add r13,-8
  add r13,10
  mov [p_item],r13
  add r13,8
  add r13,-10
  add rdx,10
  add rcx,10
  jmp return

p_item:
dq 0
p_iinfo:
dq 0

INJECT_ItemEdit+8:
  jmp newmem
  nop 3
return:

              <CheatEntries>
                <CheatEntry>
                  <ID>1337325312</ID>
                  <Description>"Dump To File (Requires The Dumper To Be Initialized First)"</Description>
                  <LastState/>
                  <VariableType>Auto Assembler Script</VariableType>
                  <AssemblerScript>{$lua}
[ENABLE]
HoverNameDumpArray={};
HoverNameDumpTimer=createTimer()
HoverNameDumpTimer.setInterval(50)
HoverNameDumpTimer.setOnTimer(function()
local p_iinfo=GetAddressSafe("[p_iinfo]");
local PartStringAddress=GetAddressSafe("[[p_item]+0xA0]");
local Type=GetAddressSafe("[[p_iinfo]+0x68]");
local WeaponType=GetAddressSafe("[[p_iinfo]+0x80]");
local ManufacturerWeaponType=GetAddressSafe("[[p_iinfo]+0x98]");
local ItemName=GetAddressSafe("[[p_iinfo]+0xB8]");
local Rarity=GetAddressSafe("[[p_iinfo]+0x108]");
local BulletType=GetAddressSafe("[[p_iinfo]+0x190]");
local Level=GetAddressSafe("[p_iinfo]+0x44");
local Price=GetAddressSafe("[p_iinfo]+0x34");
if PartStringAddress and Type and Type~=0 and WeaponType and ManufacturerWeaponType and ItemName and Rarity then
if HoverNameDumpArray[PartStringAddress]~=nil then;return;end
local PartString=readString(PartStringAddress,256);
Type=readString(Type,256,true);
WeaponType=readString(WeaponType,256,true);
ManufacturerWeaponType=readString(ManufacturerWeaponType,256,true);
ItemName=readString(ItemName,256,true);
Rarity=readString(Rarity,256,true);
BulletType=readString(BulletType,256,true);
Level=readInteger(Level);
Price=readInteger(Price);

-- Store in array to prevent duplicates
HoverNameDumpArray[PartStringAddress]={PartString=PartString,Type=Type,WeaponType=WeaponType,ManufacturerWeaponType=ManufacturerWeaponType,ItemName=ItemName,Rarity=Rarity,BulletType=BulletType,Level=Level,Price=Price};

-- Create filename based on WeaponType, replace invalid characters
local safeWeaponType = WeaponType:gsub("[^%w%-_]", "_") -- Replace non-alphanumeric chars with underscore
local filename = "GunCodes_" .. safeWeaponType .. ".txt"

local Parts=ReadPointer(p_iinfo + 0x228);
local PartsCount=readInteger(p_iinfo + 0x230);
local PartsMax=readInteger(p_iinfo + 0x234);
local PartType,PartName,InnerPartTyp=nil;
local DecodedPartString="";
local P=0;
for P=0,PartsCount,1 do
 local ReadPointer=ReadPointer(Parts+(P*8));
 if not ReadPointer then;break;end
 local InnerPartTypeId=ReadInteger( ReadPointer+0x20);
 local InnerPartType=UE.GetName(InnerPartTypeId);
 local PartTypeId=ReadInteger( ReadPointer+0x40);
 local PartType=UE.GetName(PartTypeId);
 local PartId=ReadInteger( readPointer(ReadPointer+0x68));
 local PartName=UE.GetName(PartId);
 PartType=UE.IsValidString(PartType) and PartType or nil;
 PartName=UE.IsValidString(PartName) and PartName or nil;
 InnerPartType=UE.IsValidString(InnerPartType) and InnerPartType or nil;
 if PartName and PartType then;
  DecodedPartString=DecodedPartString..PartType.."."..PartName..", ";
 elseif InnerPartType then
  DecodedPartString=DecodedPartString..InnerPartType..", ";
 end;
end


-- Prepare data to write
local dataLine = string.format("PartString: %s | Type: %s | Level: %i | Price: %i | WeaponType: %s | ManufacturerWeaponType: %s | ItemName: %s | Rarity: %s | BulletType: %s | DecodedPartString: %s | Timestamp: %s\n",
    PartString or "N/A",
    Type or "N/A",
    Level or 0,
    Price or 0,
    WeaponType or "N/A",
    ManufacturerWeaponType or "N/A",
    ItemName or "N/A",
    Rarity or "N/A",
    BulletType or "N/A",
    DecodedPartString,
    os.date("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
)
print(dataLine);

-- Append to file
local file = io.open(filename, "a") -- Open in append mode
if file then
    -- Add header if file is new (check if file is empty)
    file:seek("end", 0)
    local fileSize = file:seek()
    if fileSize == 0 then
        file:write("=== Gun Codes Dump for " .. WeaponType .. " ===\n")
        file:write("Generated: " .. os.date("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S") .. "\n")
        file:write("Format: PartString | Type | WeaponType | ManufacturerWeaponType | ItemName | Rarity | BulletType | DecodedPartString | Timestamp\n")
        file:write("================================================================================\n\n")
    end

    file:write(dataLine)
    file:close()

    print("Gun data appended to: " .. filename)
else
    print("Error: Could not open file " .. filename .. " for writing")
end

end
end);
HoverNameDumpTimer.setEnabled(true);
[DISABLE]
HoverNameDumpTimer.setEnabled(false);
HoverNameDumpTimer.destroy();
HoverNameDumpTimer=nil;
</AssemblerScript>
                </CheatEntry>
                <CheatEntry>
                  <ID>1337326701</ID>
                  <Description>"Remove dupes"</Description>
                  <LastState/>
                  <VariableType>Auto Assembler Script</VariableType>
                  <AssemblerScript>{$lua}
[ENABLE]
-- Duplicate Entry Remover for Gun Codes Dump Files
-- This script removes duplicate entries from GunCodes_*.txt files
-- Duplicates are identified by PartString, keeping the most recent entry

function removeDuplicatesFromFile(filename)
    print("Processing file: " .. filename)

    local file = io.open(filename, "r")
    if not file then
        print("Error: Could not open file " .. filename .. " for reading")
        return false
    end

    local lines = {}
    local entries = {}
    local header = {}
    local headerEnded = false

    -- Read all lines
    for line in file:lines() do
        table.insert(lines, line)
    end
    file:close()

    -- Separate header from data entries
    for i, line in ipairs(lines) do
        if not headerEnded then
            if line:match("^PartString:") then
                headerEnded = true
                -- This is the first data line
                table.insert(entries, {line = line, lineNum = i})
            else
                table.insert(header, line)
            end
        else
            if line:match("^PartString:") then
                table.insert(entries, {line = line, lineNum = i})
            end
        end
    end

    print("Found " .. #entries .. " data entries in " .. filename)

    if #entries == 0 then
        print("No data entries found in " .. filename)
        return true
    end

    -- Parse entries and remove duplicates
    local uniqueEntries = {}
    local partStringMap = {}

    for _, entry in ipairs(entries) do
        local line = entry.line
        local partString = line:match("PartString: ([^|]*)")

        if partString then
            partString = partString:trim() -- Remove whitespace

            if partStringMap[partString] then
                -- Duplicate found, keep the newer one (later in file)
                print("Duplicate PartString found: " .. partString .. " (keeping newer entry)")
                uniqueEntries[partStringMap[partString]] = nil -- Remove old entry
            end

            partStringMap[partString] = #uniqueEntries + 1
            table.insert(uniqueEntries, line)
        end
    end

    local duplicatesRemoved = #entries - #uniqueEntries
    print("Removed " .. duplicatesRemoved .. " duplicate entries from " .. filename)

    if duplicatesRemoved &gt; 0 then
        -- Write the cleaned file
        local outputFile = io.open(filename, "w")
        if not outputFile then
            print("Error: Could not open file " .. filename .. " for writing")
            return false
        end

        -- Write header
        for _, headerLine in ipairs(header) do
            outputFile:write(headerLine .. "\n")
        end

        -- Write unique entries
        for _, entry in ipairs(uniqueEntries) do
            outputFile:write(entry .. "\n")
        end

        outputFile:close()
        print("Successfully cleaned " .. filename .. " - " .. #uniqueEntries .. " unique entries remain")
    else
        print("No duplicates found in " .. filename)
    end

    return true
end

function getAllGunCodesFiles()
    local files = {}
    local handle = io.popen('dir /b GunCodes_*.txt 2&gt;nul') -- Windows command

    if handle then
        for filename in handle:lines() do
            table.insert(files, filename)
        end
        handle:close()
    else
        -- Fallback: try common patterns
        local commonTypes = {"Pistol", "Rifle", "Shotgun", "SMG", "Sniper", "Launcher", "Heavy"}
        for _, weaponType in ipairs(commonTypes) do
            local filename = "GunCodes_" .. weaponType .. ".txt"
            local testFile = io.open(filename, "r")
            if testFile then
                testFile:close()
                table.insert(files, filename)
            end
        end
    end

    return files
end

function removeAllDuplicates()
    print("=== Gun Codes Duplicate Remover ===")
    print("Scanning for GunCodes_*.txt files...")

    local files = getAllGunCodesFiles()

    if #files == 0 then
        print("No GunCodes_*.txt files found in current directory")
        return
    end

    print("Found " .. #files .. " file(s) to process:")
    for _, filename in ipairs(files) do
        print("  - " .. filename)
    end
    print()

    local totalProcessed = 0
    local totalSuccess = 0

    for _, filename in ipairs(files) do
        totalProcessed = totalProcessed + 1
        if removeDuplicatesFromFile(filename) then
            totalSuccess = totalSuccess + 1
        end
        print() -- Empty line for readability
    end

    print("=== Summary ===")
    print("Files processed: " .. totalProcessed)
    print("Files successfully cleaned: " .. totalSuccess)
    print("Duplicate removal complete!")
end

-- String trim function (Lua doesn't have built-in trim)
function string:trim()
    return self:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
end

print("Duplicates are identified by PartString, keeping the most recent entry")

--Player To Copy From
local State=UE.LocalPlayer.PlayerStateAddress;
if not UE.ArrayAlgo or not State or not ArrayOffset then;return;end
local IActiveSlot=readInteger(State+getAddressSafe("OakPlayerState.ActiveWeaponEquipSlot"));
local ActiveMemory=nil;
UE.ArrayAlgo(State,ArrayOffset,ArrayOffset+8,0x150,function(A,C)
if readByte(A+0x10D)==IActiveSlot then
ActiveMemory=readBytes(A,0x150,true);
return true;
end
return false;
end);
if not ActiveMemory then;
print("Failed To Find The Users Active Weapon!");return;
end
--Copy To Players Bank:
UE.ExtendMemoryArray(UE.LocalPlayer.PlayerStateAddress,ArrayOffset,ArrayOffset+8,ArrayOffset+12,0x150,1500,function(A,C,M)
writeBytes(A,ActiveMemory);
--Write Index's Into The New Weapon/Item In The Inventory
writeInteger(A,C+1);
writeInteger(A+0x10,C+1);
writeInteger(A+0x108,C+1);
writeByte(A+0x10D,255);--Free Slot
local Str=readString(readPointer(M+0xB8),1000);
local ST_=AllocateMemory(1000);
writePointer(A+0xB8,ST_);
writeString(ST_,Str);
end);
print("Successfully Duped That Players Weapon From Slot: "..IActiveSlot);
memrec.Active = false;
end)

[ENABLE]
BankItemsRecordList=UE.MemoryRecordList(memrec,"Bank Items","[[[[[GEngine+0x1358]+0x38]]+0x30]+0x398]",0xB08,0xB10,0x150,function(Hdr,i,OFFSET,createEntry);
local PS=nil;
local E=createEntry(Hdr, "Slot "..i)
E.Address=i ==0 and "+0" or string.format("+0x%X",OFFSET*i);
E.IsAddressGroupHeader=true;
createEntry(E, "ReplicationID", 0,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "ReplicationKey", 4,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "MostRecentArrayReplicationKey", 8,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "InstanceId", 0x10,vtDword);

createEntry(E, "Type Pointer", 0x18,vtQword).ShowAsHex=true;
--createEntry(TypePtr, "RawType", 0x20,vtCustom,UE.Type_FName);
PS=createEntry(E, "ObjectType", 0x18,vtCustom,UE.Type_FName);
PS.setOffsetCount(1);
PS.setOffset(0, 0x3C);

PS=createEntry(E, "ObjectInternalType", 0x18,vtCustom,UE.Type_FName);
PS.setOffsetCount(1);
PS.setOffset(0, 0x58);

createEntry(E, "Info Pointer", 0x20,vtQword).ShowAsHex=true;
--createEntry(TypePtr, "RawType", 0x20,vtCustom,UE.Type_FName);
PS=createEntry(E, "Name", 0x20,vtCustom,UE.Type_FName);
PS.setOffsetCount(1);
PS.setOffset(0, 0x48);

PS=createEntry(E, "Info", 0x20,vtCustom,UE.Type_FName);
PS.setOffsetCount(1);
PS.setOffset(0, 0x60);


createEntry(E, "?Pointer", 0x28,vtQword).ShowAsHex=true;


createEntry(E, "Parts String Pointer", 0xB8,vtQword).ShowAsHex=true;
PS=createEntry(E, "Parts String", 0xB8,vtString,256);
PS.setOffsetCount(1);
PS.setOffset(0, 0);
--createEntry(E, "PartString.Count", 0xC0,vtDword);
--createEntry(E, "PartString.Max", 0xC4,vtDword);

createEntry(E, "Quantity", 0xF8,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "Flags", 0xFC,vtDword);

createEntry(E, "Handle", 0x108,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "Flags2", 0x10C,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "EquipSlot", 0x10D,vtByte);
createEntry(E, "SummaryHash", 0x110,vtDword);
--createEntry(E, "InlineTokens.TokenCount", 0x114,vtDword);
--createEntry(E, "InlineTokens.Hash", 0x118,vtDword);
--createEntry(E, "InlineTokens.Name", 0x11C,vtDword);
--createEntry(E, "ExternalTokens", 0x128,vtPointer);
--createEntry(E, "ExternalTokens.Count", 0x130,vtDword);
--createEntry(E, "ExternalTokens.Max", 0x134,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "MaxQuantity", 0x138,vtDword);
createEntry(E, "IsLocked", 0x13C,vtByte);
end);

[DISABLE]
if BankItemsRecordList then
UE.AddressListBeginUpdate();
pcall(memoryrecord_delete,BankItemsRecordList)
UE.AddressListEndUpdate();

end

[ENABLE]
CreateThread(function()
local Skills=GetAddressSafe("[[[[[GEngine+0x1358]+0x38]]+0x30]+0x3D0]");
if not Skills then
memrec.Active = false;
printf("Cannot Find The Skills");
return
end
local B=readInteger(Skills+0x6DF8);
local A=readPointer(Skills+0x6DF0);
local C=0;
local D=0;
local E=0;
local F=0;local G=0;
print("Total Trees: "..B);
for C=0,B,1 do
D=readPointer(A+(0x8*C));
if D then
E=UE.GetName(readInteger(D+0x108));
if E then
local Nodes=ReadPointer(D+0x138);
local NodesC=ReadInteger(D+0x140);
G=0;
for F=0,NodesC-1,1 do
writeByte(Nodes+G+0x90,1);
writeByte(Nodes+G+0x94,1);
writeByte(Nodes+G+0x91,1);
writeInteger(Nodes+G+0x98,999);
writeInteger(Nodes+G+0x9C,999);
G=G+0xA0+0x8;
end

local Groups=ReadPointer(D+0x148);
local GroupsC=ReadInteger(D+0x150);
G=0;
for F=0,GroupsC-1,1 do
writeByte(Groups+G+0x80,1);
G=UE.AlignOffset(G+0x81);
--print(string.format(E.." 0x%X",G));
end
print(string.format("%s Group Count: %i",E,GroupsC));
end
end
end
memrec.Active = false;
end)
[DISABLE]

---- Table File Package Loader
function tableFilePackageLoader(name, modPath);local tableFile = findTableFile(modPath);
if tableFile then;local stream = tableFile.getData();if stream then;
local fileStr = readStringLocal(stream.memory, stream.size);if fileStr then;
local status, ret = pcall(load, fileStr, modPath);
if not status then print(ret)return; end;
if ret ==nil then;
local F,E=autoAssembleCheck("{$lua}\n"..fileStr,false);
if not F then;
if string.find(E,"&lt;%\\239&gt;") then;E=E..", Failed To Load UTF8 Script, Please Save In Ansi Format";end
print("Failed To Load LUA Script: "..name.."\n"..E);
ERROR=E;
end
return nil;
else
return ret(name, modPath);end;end;end;
end;
print(string.format('Error loading table module: %s : %s', name, modPath));
end
function tableFilePackageSearcher(name);local err = '';local mod_paths = { name..'.lua', name..'.init.lua' };local tableFile, modPath;for i, path in ipairs(mod_paths) do;tableFile = findTableFile(path);if tableFile then;modPath = path;break;else;err = err..string.format("\n\tno table file '%s'", path);end;end;if tableFile and modPath then;return tableFilePackageLoader, modPath;end;return err;end;
if not TABLE_LUA_PACKAGE_SEARCHER_LOADED then;if RELEASE_MODE then;table.insert(package.searchers, 2, tableFilePackageSearcher);else;table.insert(package.searchers, tableFilePackageSearcher);end;TABLE_LUA_PACKAGE_SEARCHER_LOADED = true;end
if not REQUIRE_BYPASS_LOADED then;local _require = require;function require(name);if REREQUIRE or RerequireList and RerequireList[name] then;package.loaded[name] = false;end;local status, ret = pcall(_require, name);if status then;return ret;else;local err = ret:gsub('\n', '\r\n'):gsub('.dllC:\\', ".dll'\r\n\tno file 'C:\\");error(err, 2);end;end;REQUIRE_BYPASS_LOADED = true;end

--REALLY BAD BREAKPOINT, A WAY TO BREAKPOINT SOMEWHAT WITHOUT DEBUG ACCESS, NOTE THIS SUCKS BAD!
if not RBBPMEMVIEW_FARJUMP then;
 Memview=getMemoryViewForm();
 RBBP_ENABLED={};
 RBBP_ENABLED_I={};
 RSBP_JUMPCODE=[[
alloc(RBBP_ALLOC,$1000,INSTRUCTIONADDRESS)
label(HERE RBBP_HIT RBBP_RAX RBBP_RBX RBBP_RCX RBBP_RDX RBBP_RSI RBBP_RDI RBBP_RBP RBBP_RSP RBBP_R8 RBBP_R9 RBBP_R10 RBBP_R11 RBBP_R12 RBBP_R13 RBBP_R14 RBBP_R15 RBBP_RIP return)
RBBP_ALLOC:
ORIGINALCODE
  cmp [RBBP_HIT],0
  jne return
  mov [RBBP_HIT],1
  mov [RBBP_RAX],rax
  mov [RBBP_RBX],rbx
  mov [RBBP_RCX],rcx
  mov [RBBP_RDX],rdx
  mov [RBBP_RSI],rsi
  mov [RBBP_RDI],rdi
  mov [RBBP_RBP],rbp
  mov [RBBP_RSP],rsp
  mov [RBBP_R8],r8
  mov [RBBP_R9],r9
  mov [RBBP_R10],r10
  mov [RBBP_R11],r11
  mov [RBBP_R12],r12
  mov [RBBP_R13],r13
  mov [RBBP_R14],r14
  mov [RBBP_R15],r15
  HERE:
  cmp [RBBP_HIT],0
  jne HERE
  jmp return

RBBP_HIT:
dq 0
RBBP_RAX:
dq 0
RBBP_RBX:
dq 0
RBBP_RCX:
dq 0
RBBP_RDX:
dq 0
RBBP_RSI:
dq 0
RBBP_RDI:
dq 0
RBBP_RBP:
dq 0
RBBP_RSP:
dq 0
RBBP_R8:
dq 0
RBBP_R9:
dq 0
RBBP_R10:
dq 0
RBBP_R11:
dq 0
RBBP_R12:
dq 0
RBBP_R13:
dq 0
RBBP_R14:
dq 0
RBBP_R15:
dq 0
RBBP_RIP:
dq 0

INSTRUCTIONADDRESS:
  jmp RBBP_ALLOC
  nops
return:
registersymbol(RBBP_ALLOC RBBP_HIT RBBP_RAX RBBP_RBX RBBP_RCX RBBP_RDX RBBP_RSI RBBP_RDI RBBP_RBP RBBP_RSP RBBP_R8 RBBP_R9 RBBP_R10 RBBP_R11 RBBP_R12 RBBP_R13 RBBP_R14 RBBP_R15 RBBP_RIP)
]];
 RBBP_DEALLOCFUNC=function();
  local A=Memview.DisassemblerView.SelectedAddress;
  writeByte(string.gsub( "RBBP_HIT","%RBBP_",string.format("RBBP_0x%X_",A)),0);
  sleep(2);--Wait till near next tick to dealloc ect
  writeBytes(A,RBBP_ENABLED[A].OrignalBytes);
  local Allocated=GetAddressSafe(string.format("RBBP_0x%X_ALLOC",A));
  local AAScript=string.gsub("unregistersymbol(RBBP_ALLOC RBBP_HIT RBBP_RAX RBBP_RBX RBBP_RCX RBBP_RDX RBBP_RSI RBBP_RDI RBBP_RBP RBBP_RSP RBBP_R8 RBBP_R9 RBBP_R10 RBBP_R11 RBBP_R12 RBBP_R13 RBBP_R14 RBBP_R15 RBBP_RIP)",
  "%RBBP_",string.format("RBBP_0x%X_",A));
  AutoAssemble(AAScript);
  if Allocated then
   deAlloc(Allocated);
  end
  RBBP_ENABLED[A]=nil;
end
 local function Create_MainMenuItem ( MainMenu, Caption, Name, Position, OnClick )
  local MenuItem = createMenuItem( MainMenu )
  MenuItem.Caption = Caption
  MenuItem.Name = Name
  MenuItem.OnClick = OnClick
  MainMenu.Items.Insert( Position or MainMenu.Items.Count, MenuItem )
  return MenuItem
 end
 RBBPMEMVIEW_JUMP= Create_MainMenuItem( Memview.debuggerpopup, 'Really Bad Breakpoint (Jump)', nil, nil, function();
  local Count=5;
  local A=Memview.DisassemblerView.SelectedAddress;
  if not RBBP_ENABLED[A] then;
   local FS=0;
   local Original_Instructions="";
   while FS&lt;Count+1 do
    local O=getInstructionSize(A+FS);
    local F____,Opcode=splitDisassembledString(disassemble(A+FS))
    Original_Instructions=Original_Instructions..Opcode.."\n";
    FS=FS+O;
   end;
   RBBP_ENABLED[A]={OrignalBytes=ReadBytes(A,FS,true),Seen=false};
   RBBP_ENABLED_I[#RBBP_ENABLED_I+1]=A;
   local AAScript=RSBP_JUMPCODE;
   local NOPCOUNT=(#RBBP_ENABLED[A].OrignalBytes)-Count;
   --printf("0x%X: Size: %i, Original_Instructions: \n%s\nNOPCOUNT: %i",A,FS,Original_Instructions,NOPCOUNT);
   local NOPS=NOPCOUNT&lt;=0 and "" or NOPCOUNT&gt;1 and string.format("nop %i",NOPCOUNT) or "nop";
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%RBBP_",string.format("RBBP_0x%X_",A));
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%ORIGINALCODE",Original_Instructions);
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%INSTRUCTIONADDRESS",string.format("%X",A));
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%nops",NOPS);
   local S,E=autoAssembleCheck(AAScript, false);
   if S then;
    AutoAssemble(AAScript);
    Memview.DisassemblerView.SelectedAddress=getAddressSafe(string.format("RBBP_0x%X_ALLOC",A));
   else
    print("RBBP Error:\n"..E.."\n"..AAScript);
   end
  else
   RBBP_DEALLOCFUNC();
  end
 end)
 RBBPMEMVIEW_FARJUMP= Create_MainMenuItem( Memview.debuggerpopup, 'Really Bad Breakpoint (Far Jump)', nil, nil, function();
  local Count=14;
  local A=Memview.DisassemblerView.SelectedAddress;
  if not RBBP_ENABLED[A] then;
   local FS=0;
   local Original_Instructions="";
   while FS&lt;Count+1 do
    local O=getInstructionSize(A+FS);
    local F____,Opcode=splitDisassembledString(disassemble(A+FS))
    Original_Instructions=Original_Instructions..Opcode.."\n";
    FS=FS+O;
   end;
   --printf("0x%X: Size: %i, Original_Instructions: \n%s",A,FS,Original_Instructions);
   RBBP_ENABLED[A]={OrignalBytes=ReadBytes(A,FS,true),Seen=false};
   RBBP_ENABLED_I[#RBBP_ENABLED_I+1]=A;
   local AAScript=string.gsub( RSBP_JUMPCODE,"%jmp RBBP_ALLOC","jmp far RBBP_ALLOC");
   local NOPCOUNT=(#RBBP_ENABLED[A].OrignalBytes)-Count;
   local NOPS=NOPCOUNT&lt;=0 and "" or NOPCOUNT&gt;1 and string.format("nop %i",NOPCOUNT) or "nop";
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%RBBP_",string.format("RBBP_0x%X_",A));
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%ORIGINALCODE",Original_Instructions);
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%INSTRUCTIONADDRESS",string.format("%X",A));
   AAScript=string.gsub( AAScript,"%nops",NOPS);
   local S,E=autoAssembleCheck(AAScript, false);
   if S then;
    AutoAssemble(AAScript);
    Memview.DisassemblerView.SelectedAddress=getAddressSafe(string.format("RBBP_0x%X_ALLOC",A));
   else
    print("RBBP Error:\n"..E.."\n"..AAScript);
   end
  else
   RBBP_DEALLOCFUNC();
  end
 end)

 local NHARegisters=createPanel(Memview.Splitter2.Parent)
 NHARegisters.Visible=false;
 NHARegisters.Align="alRight"
 NHARegisters.Width=170
 NHARegisters.BaseCaption={};
 NHARegisters.Left=Memview.Splitter2.Left+Memview.Splitter2.Width+2
 NHARegisters.CloseButton=createButton(NHARegisters)
 NHARegisters.CloseButton.Align="alTop"
 NHARegisters.CloseButton.Caption="Close";
 NHARegisters.CloseButton.OnClick=function()
  Memview.Splitter2.Visible=false
  if Memview.NHARegisters then
   Memview.NHARegisters.Visible=false
  end
 end
 NHARegisters.Labels=createPanel(NHARegisters)
 NHARegisters.Labels.Align="alClient"
 local SZE=17;local Vert=0;
 local CreateRegisterLabel=function(Name)
  local LBL=createPanel(NHARegisters.Labels)
  LBL.Align="alTop"
  LBL.Top=Vert
  LBL.Height=SZE
  LBL.Name=Name;
  if #Name==2 or Name=="RSI" then
   LBL.BaseCaption=Name..":   0x%08X";
  elseif Name=="RDI" then
   LBL.BaseCaption=Name..":  0x%08X";
  else
   LBL.BaseCaption=Name..": 0x%08X";
  end
  LBL.Caption=string.format(LBL.BaseCaption,0);
  NHARegisters.BaseCaption[LBL.Name]=LBL.BaseCaption;
  LBL.Alignment = "taLeftJustify"
  LBL.Layout = "tlCenter"
  LBL.AutoSize=false
  LBL.BorderStyle="bsNone";
  LBL.Hint = "Click To Copy Address To Clipboard"
  LBL.ShowHint = LBL.Hint ~= ""
  LBL.BorderSpacing.Left=5;
  LBL.BorderWidth=-1;
  LBL.BevelColor=LBL.Color
  LBL.Cursor=crHandPoint
  LBL.Font=Memview.Font
  LBL.OnClick=function();
   local CAP=stringToByteTable(LBL.Caption);
   local C=1;local Seen_=0;
   while C&lt;#CAP do
    if Seen_==0 then
     if string.char(CAP[C])==":" then
      Seen_=1;
     end
    elseif Seen_==1 then
     if string.char(CAP[C])~=" " then
      Seen_=2;
      break;
     end
   end
   C=C+1;
   end
   local R= byteTableToString(CAP,C);
   writeToClipboard(R)
  end
  Vert=Vert+SZE;
 end

 RBBP_SetRegisters=function(RAX,RBX,RCX,RDX,RSI,RDI,RBP,RSP,R8,R9,R10,R11,R12,R13,R14,R15,RIP)
  local Ar=Memview.NHARegisters.Labels.Control;
  local Nm=Memview.NHARegisters.BaseCaption;
  Ar[1].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[1].Name],RAX);
  Ar[2].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[2].Name],RCX);
  Ar[3].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[3].Name],RDX);
  Ar[4].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[4].Name],RSI);
  Ar[5].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[5].Name],RDI);
  Ar[6].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[6].Name],RBP);
  Ar[7].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[7].Name],RSP);
  Ar[8].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[8].Name],R8);
  Ar[9].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[9].Name],R9);
  Ar[10].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[10].Name],R10);
  Ar[11].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[11].Name],R11);
  Ar[12].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[12].Name],R12);
  Ar[13].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[13].Name],R13);
  Ar[14].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[14].Name],R14);
  Ar[15].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[15].Name],R15);
  Ar[16].Caption=string.format(Nm[Ar[16].Name],RIP);
  Memview.Splitter2.Visible=true
  Memview.NHARegisters.Visible=true
 end

 OnPopupOld=Memview.debuggerpopup.OnPopup
 Memview.debuggerpopup.OnPopup=function(...)
  OnPopupOld(...)
  local State=RBBP_ENABLED[Memview.DisassemblerView.SelectedAddress]
  RBBPMEMVIEW_FARJUMP.Visible=not State;
  if not State then
   local Base=State and "Disable Really Bad Breakpoint" or "Enable Really Bad Breakpoint"
   RBBPMEMVIEW_JUMP.Caption=Base.." (Jump 5 Bytes)"
   RBBPMEMVIEW_FARJUMP.Caption=Base.." (Far Jump 14 Bytes)"
  else
  RBBPMEMVIEW_JUMP.Caption="Disable Really Bad Breakpoint"
  end
 end

 RunButton= Memview.tbDebug.getControl(2);
 if not RunButtonOldClick then
  RunButtonOldClick=RunButton.OnClick;
  RunButton.OnClick=function(...);
   local A;
   for A=1,#RBBP_ENABLED_I,1 do
    local Address=RBBP_ENABLED_I[A];
    if RBBP_ENABLED[Address] and RBBP_ENABLED[Address].Seen and readByte(string.format("RBBP_0x%X_HIT",Address))==1 then
     writeByte(string.format("RBBP_0x%X_HIT",Address),0);
     Memview.tbDebug.Visible=false
     RunButton.Enabled=false;
     RBBP_ENABLED[Address].Seen=false;
    end
   end
   RunButtonOldClick(...);
  end
 end

 MainFormTimerHijack=function();
  local C=#RBBP_ENABLED_I;
  if C&gt;0 then
   local A;
   for A=1,#RBBP_ENABLED_I,1 do
    local Address=RBBP_ENABLED_I[A];
    local Formatted=string.format("RBBP_0x%X_",Address);
    if RBBP_ENABLED[Address] and not RBBP_ENABLED[Address].Seen and readByte(Formatted.."HIT")==1 then
     RBBP_ENABLED[Address].Seen=true;
     Memview.DisassemblerView.SelectedAddress=getAddressSafe(Formatted.."ALLOC");
     Memview.tbDebug.Visible=true
     RunButton.Enabled=true;
     RBBP_SetRegisters(readPointer(Formatted.."RAX"),readPointer(Formatted.."RBX"),readPointer(Formatted.."RCX"),readPointer(Formatted.."RDX"),
     readPointer(Formatted.."RSI"),readPointer(Formatted.."RDI"),readPointer(Formatted.."RBP"),readPointer(Formatted.."RSP"),
     readPointer(Formatted.."R8"),readPointer(Formatted.."R9"),readPointer(Formatted.."R10"),readPointer(Formatted.."R11"),readPointer(Formatted.."R12"),
     readPointer(Formatted.."R13"),readPointer(Formatted.."R14"),readPointer(Formatted.."R15"),readPointer(Formatted.."RIP"));
    end
   end
  end
 end
 if not MainFormTimerOg then
  local I=0;
  for I=0,MainForm.ComponentCount,1 do
   if MainForm.Component[I].ClassName=="TTimer" and MainForm.Component[I].Enabled and MainForm.Component[I].OnTimer then
    MainFormTimerOg=MainForm.Component[I].OnTimer;
    MainFormTimer=MainForm.Component[I];
    MainForm.Component[I].OnTimer=function(...);
     MainFormTimerHijack();
     MainFormTimerOg(...);
    end;
    break
   end
  end
 end
end;
